4a:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":"The key concept of validation feedback strategy is, let LLM function calling to construct invalid typed arguments first, and informing detailed type errors to the LLM, so that induce LLM to emend the wrong typed arguments at the next turn. In this way, I could uprise the success rate of function calling from 30% to 99% just by one step validation feedback. Even though the LLM is still occurs type error, it always has been caught at the next turn."}]
